{\footnotesize\ttfamily \#define AL\+\_\+\+BUFFERS\+\_\+\+PROCESSED~0x1016}

Source Buffer Queue processed count (query only). Type\+: ALint

The number of queued buffers that have been fully processed, and can be removed with al\+Source\+Unqueue\+Buffers.

Looping sources will never fully process buffers because they will be set to play again for when the source loops. \Hypertarget{al_8h_aa8e86763ae91cb00dbb4344506eef6fe}\label{al_8h_aa8e86763ae91cb00dbb4344506eef6fe}

Outer cone angle, in degrees. Range\+: \mbox{[}0 -\/ 360\mbox{]} Default\+: 360

The angle covered by the outer cone, where the source will be fully attenuated. \Hypertarget{al_8h_a180bb7a95732296a95592d99ab7a1687}\label{al_8h_a180bb7a95732296a95592d99ab7a1687}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \#define AL\+\_\+\+CONE\+\_\+\+OUTER\+\_\+\+GAIN~0x1022}

Outer cone gain. Type\+: ALfloat Range\+: \mbox{[}0.\+0 -\/ 1.\+0\mbox{]} Default\+: 0.\+0

The gain attenuation applied when the listener is outside of the source\textquotesingle{}s outer cone. \Hypertarget{al_8h_a8bbb95b3a1bc814da897d5dfe2a1712a}\label{al_8h_a8bbb95b3a1bc814da897d5dfe2a1712a}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{AL\_DIRECTION}{AL\_DIRECTION}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \#define AL\+\_\+\+DIRECTION~0x1005}

Source direction. Type\+: ALfloat\mbox{[}3\mbox{]}, ALint\mbox{[}3\mbox{]} Default\+: \{0, 0, 0\}

Specifies the current direction in local space. A zero-\/length vector specifies an omni-\/directional source (cone is ignored). \Hypertarget{al_8h_a04cb8d5a824c2b49f26523995c4ecd29}\label{al_8h_a04cb8d5a824c2b49f26523995c4ecd29} 
\index{al.h@{al.h}!AL\_DISTANCE\_MODEL@{AL\_DISTANCE\_MODEL}}
\index{AL\_DISTANCE\_MODEL@{AL\_DISTANCE\_MODEL}!al.h@{al.h}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{AL\_DISTANCE\_MODEL}{AL\_DISTANCE\_MODEL}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \#define AL\+\_\+\+DISTANCE\+\_\+\+MODEL~0x\+D000}

Distance attenuation model. Type\+: ALint Range\+: \mbox{[}AL\+\_\+\+NONE, AL\+\_\+\+INVERSE\+\_\+\+DISTANCE, AL\+\_\+\+INVERSE\+\_\+\+DISTANCE\+\_\+\+CLAMPED, AL\+\_\+\+LINEAR\+\_\+\+DISTANCE, AL\+\_\+\+LINEAR\+\_\+\+DISTANCE\+\_\+\+CLAMPED, AL\+\_\+\+EXPONENT\+\_\+\+DISTANCE, AL\+\_\+\+EXPONENT\+\_\+\+DISTANCE\+\_\+\+CLAMPED\mbox{]} Default\+: AL\+\_\+\+INVERSE\+\_\+\+DISTANCE\+\_\+\+CLAMPED

The model by which sources attenuate with distance.

None -\/ No distance attenuation. Inverse -\/ Doubling the distance halves the source gain. Linear -\/ Linear gain scaling between the reference and max distances. Exponent -\/ Exponential gain dropoff.

Clamped variations work like the non-\/clamped counterparts, except the distance calculated is clamped between the reference and max distances. \Hypertarget{al_8h_aef68e4f99022c27c2d8fb3f08b44c3e2}\label{al_8h_aef68e4f99022c27c2d8fb3f08b44c3e2}

\index{AL\_DOPPLER\_FACTOR@{AL\_DOPPLER\_FACTOR}!al.h@{al.h}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{AL\_DOPPLER\_FACTOR}{AL\_DOPPLER\_FACTOR}}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \#define AL\+\_\+\+GAIN~0x100A}

Source or listener gain. Type\+: ALfloat Range\+: \mbox{[}0.\+0 -\/ \mbox{]}

A value of 1.\+0 means unattenuated. Each division by 2 equals an attenuation of about -\/6dB. Each multiplicaton by 2 equals an amplification of about +6dB.

A value of 0.\+0 is meaningless with respect to a logarithmic scale; it is silent. \Hypertarget{al_8h_a711d1c38cf7baddd4ecf66ab63ccf5d9}\label{al_8h_a711d1c38cf7baddd4ecf66ab63ccf5d9}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{AL\_POSITION}{AL\_POSITION}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \#define AL\+\_\+\+POSITION~0x1004}

Source or listener position. Type\+: ALfloat\mbox{[}3\mbox{]}, ALint\mbox{[}3\mbox{]} Default\+: \{0, 0, 0\}

The source or listener location in three dimensional space.

Open\+AL, like Open\+GL, uses a right handed coordinate system, where in a frontal default view X (thumb) points right, Y points up (index finger), and Z points towards the viewer/camera (middle finger).

To switch from a left handed coordinate system, flip the sign on the Z coordinate. \Hypertarget{al_8h_a63b94dbf55962c548e126b34b86feec8}\label{al_8h_a63b94dbf55962c548e126b34b86feec8}

Multiplier to exaggerate or diminish distance attenuation.

At 0.\+0, no distance attenuation ever occurs. \Hypertarget{al_8h_a8f47a1f4b0d18ab9adf181825c522a75}\label{al_8h_a8f47a1f4b0d18ab9adf181825c522a75}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \#define AL\+\_\+\+SOURCE\+\_\+\+TYPE~0x1027}

Source type (query only). Type\+: ALint Range\+: \mbox{[}AL\+\_\+\+STATIC, AL\+\_\+\+STREAMING, AL\+\_\+\+UNDETERMINED\mbox{]}

A Source is Static if a Buffer has been attached using AL\+\_\+\+BUFFER.

A Source is Streaming if one or more Buffers have been attached using al\+Source\+Queue\+Buffers.

A Source is Undetermined when it has the NULL buffer attached using AL\+\_\+\+BUFFER. \Hypertarget{al_8h_a8b55e5c1a046667f4d1055d5af27f893}\label{al_8h_a8b55e5c1a046667f4d1055d5af27f893}
